    Introduction

    This documentation aims to provide all the information you need to work with our API.

    As you scroll, you'll see code examples for working with the API in different programming languages in the dark area to the right (or as part of the content on mobile). You can switch the language used with the tabs at the top right (or from the nav menu at the top left on mobile).

    Base URL

    https://api.arielnet.ir

    Authenticating requests

    Authenticate requests to this API's endpoints by sending an Authorization header with the value "Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}".

    All authenticated endpoints are marked with a requires authentication badge in the documentation below.

    You can retrieve your token by visiting your dashboard and clicking Generate API token.

    Attribute

    Display a listing of the resource.

    requires authentication

    Example request:
    curl --request GET \
    --get "https://api.arielnet.ir/api/cms/attribute" \
    --header "Authorization: Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"sort\": {
        \"column\": \"id\",
        \"order\": \"asc\"
    },
    \"page\": 1,
    \"pageLength\": 10
}"

    const url = new URL(
    "https://api.arielnet.ir/api/cms/attribute"
);

const headers = {
    "Authorization": "Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "sort": {
        "column": "id",
        "order": "asc"
    },
    "page": 1,
    "pageLength": 10
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
    $client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'https://api.arielnet.ir/api/cms/attribute',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Authorization' => 'Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}',
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
        'json' => [
            'sort' => [
                'column' => 'id',
                'order' => 'asc',
            ],
            'page' => 1,
            'pageLength' => 10,
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));
    import requests
import json

url = 'https://api.arielnet.ir/api/cms/attribute'
payload = {
    "sort": {
        "column": "id",
        "order": "asc"
    },
    "page": 1,
    "pageLength": 10
}
headers = {
  'Authorization': 'Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}',
  'Content-Type': 'application/json',
  'Accept': 'application/json'
}

response = requests.request('GET', url, headers=headers, json=payload)
response.json()

    GET api/cms/attribute

    Body Parameters

    page  integer optional

    ContactInfos Admin

    Display a listing of the contactInfos.

    requires authentication

    Example request:
    curl --request GET \
    --get "https://api.arielnet.ir/api/cms/contact-info" \
    --header "Authorization: Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"sort\": {
        \"column\": \"id\",
        \"order\": \"asc\"
    },
    \"page\": 1,
    \"pageLength\": 10,
    \"group\": \"contact\"
}"

    const url = new URL(
    "https://api.arielnet.ir/api/cms/contact-info"
);

const headers = {
    "Authorization": "Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "sort": {
        "column": "id",
        "order": "asc"
    },
    "page": 1,
    "pageLength": 10,
    "group": "contact"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
    $client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'https://api.arielnet.ir/api/cms/contact-info',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Authorization' => 'Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}',
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
        'json' => [
            'sort' => [
                'column' => 'id',
                'order' => 'asc',
            ],
            'page' => 1,
            'pageLength' => 10,
            'group' => 'contact',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

    Request      

    GET api/cms/contact-info

    Body Parameters

    sort  object optional  

    sort.column  string optional  

    Column of sorting.

    sort.order  string optional  

    Order of sorting.

    page  integer optional  

    Number of page.

    pageLength  integer optional  

    Length of page.

    group  string optional  

    Group of contact infos you prefer to show.

    Store a newly created ContactInfo in storage.

    requires authentication

    Example request:
    curl --request POST \
    "https://api.arielnet.ir/api/cms/contact-info" \
    --header "Authorization: Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"type\": \"phone\",
    \"group\": \"contact\",
    \"title\": \"company phone\",
    \"icon\": \"phone\",
    \"value\": \"983155311111\"
}"

    const url = new URL(
    "https://api.arielnet.ir/api/cms/contact-info"
);

const headers = {
    "Authorization": "Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "type": "phone",
    "group": "contact",
    "title": "company phone",
    "icon": "phone",
    "value": "983155311111"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
    $client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->post(
    'https://api.arielnet.ir/api/cms/contact-info',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Authorization' => 'Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}',
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
        'json' => [
            'type' => 'phone',

            'icon' => 'phone',
            'value' => '983155311111',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

    Request      

    POST api/cms/contact-info

    Body Parameters

    type  required optional  

    string Type of contact info.

    group  required optional  

    string Group of contact info.

    title  required optional  

    string Title of contact info.

    icon  required optional  

    string Icon of contact info.

    value  required optional  

    string Value or url of contact info.

    Display the specified contactInfo.

    requires authentication

    Example request:

    --get "https://api.arielnet.ir/api/cms/contact-info/maxime" \

    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));
    import requests
import json

url = 'https://api.arielnet.ir/api/tags'
payload = {
    "tag": "tag"
}
headers = {
  'Content-Type': 'application/json',
  'Accept': 'application/json'
}

response = requests.request('GET', url, headers=headers, json=payload)
response.json()
